      <p>To assist in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ADMINH" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:ADMINH">administration</a> of the Wikipedia community and development of the encyclopedia, the community has established a wide range of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ADMINP" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:ADMINP">administration pages</a>. Many of the pages listed below are static in nature and provide information and guidance on certain aspects of maintaining the project. Others pages are related to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Request_directory" title="Wikipedia:Request directory">Wikipedia request departments</a>, and need continuous attention from volunteers like you to answer or deal with questions and requests. For a listing of <i>ongoing discussions</i> and <i>current requests</i>, see the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Dashboard" title="Wikipedia:Dashboard">dashboard</a>. For other useful directories and indexes, see the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Directory" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Directory">directory</a>. </p>

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Editorial_departments">Editorial departments</span></h3> 
      <p>Articles are contributed and edited directly by users. All Wikipedians belong to the editorial team. </p> 
      <div> 
       <table class="multicol" role="presentation" style="border-collapse: collapse; padding: 0; border: 0; background:transparent; width:100%;">
        <tbody>
         <tr> 
          <td style="text-align: left; vertical-align: top;"> <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Content_creation">Content creation</span></h3> <p><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Tools" title="Wikipedia:Tools">Writing tools</a><br> <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Resource_Exchange" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Resource Exchange">Writing resources</a><br> <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Translation" title="Wikipedia:Translation">Article translation</a> </p> <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Article_creation"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Starting_an_article" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Starting an article">Article creation</a></span></h4> <p><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_creation" title="Wikipedia:Articles for creation">Articles for creation</a><br> <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requested_articles" title="Wikipedia:Requested articles">Article requests</a><br> <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Contribution_Team" title="Wikipedia:Contribution Team">Contribution Team</a><br> <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_feedback" title="Wikipedia:Requests for feedback">Feedback requests</a><br> <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:List_of_encyclopedia_topics" title="Wikipedia:List of encyclopedia topics">Missing articles</a><br> <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Most_wanted_articles" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Most wanted articles">Most wanted articles</a> </p> <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Article_refinement">Article refinement</span></h4> <p><a href="/wiki/Category:Recently_revised" title="Category:Recently revised">Review new overhauls</a><br> <a href="/wiki/Category:Wikipedia_articles_needing_factual_verification" title="Category:Wikipedia articles needing factual verification">Verification needed</a><br> <a id="Pictures">Pictures</span></h4> <p><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requested_pictures" title="Wikipedia:Requested pictures">Requested pictures</a> </p> <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="WikiProjects_and_teams"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject">WikiProjects</a> and teams</span></h3> <p><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Council/Directory" WikiProjects">Inactive projects</a> </p> <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Improvement_teams">Improvement teams</span></h4> <p><a href="/wiki/Template:Active_Wiki_Fixup_Projects" Editorial Team</a> </p> </td> 
          <td style="text-align: left; vertical-align: top;"> <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Maintenance"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Maintenance"       <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_communities">Related communities</span></h3> 
      <p>Wikipedia is hosted by the <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_Foundation" title="Wikimedia Foundation">Wikimedia Foundation</a>, a non-profit organization that also hosts a range of other <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Multilingual_coordination" title="Wikipedia:Multilingual coordination">multilingual</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Copyrights" title="Wikipedia:Copyrights">free-content</a> <a href="https://foundation.wikimedia.org/wiki/Our_projects" class="extiw" title="wikimedia:Our projects">projects</a>. Here are the links to their <i><b>main community pages</b></i>: </p> 
      <table width="100%" align="center" cellpadding="4" style="text-align:left; background-color: transparent;">
